msg:The hotel was clean and modern, and every single room has a view of the surrounding karst mountains. The view from the pool is to die for. 

The food in the restaurant was pretty good, if a bit overpriced. It would be lovely if they also had an English menu, but that's rare in this corner of China, and we managed with rudimentary Chinese and pointing. 

Be aware that the hotel is in the middle of nowhere. Other than a small convenience store, there's nothing around. You need a car, scooter or bike to get around.

If I had any complaints, it would be that the rooms aren't very well insulated for sound. We could hear everyone who walked up or down the staircase.

msg:The hotel there is located in the countryside on the opposite bank of the boat dock for tourists on bamboo rafts in Mingshi Pastoral Scenic Area.
When I drove to the hotel in the evening, a dignified and beautiful girl who called herself Xiaoli greeted me with enthusiasm. She actively took a look at all the room types according to our requirements. She felt very good, even better than what we saw on Ctrip.com!
Xiaoli took us through the check-in process quickly, guided us to park the car to a suitable location, and took us to the restaurant for dinner. The taste was very good, especially the spicy "Daohuaxiang" fish. I couldn't help but order again the next night!
In order to make it easier for us to start cycling to see the mountains and rivers at 6 o'clock the next morning, Xiaoli took the initiative to arrange electric bicycles overnight.
On the third day, we set off to Detian Waterfall at 7 in the morning. The breakfast at the hotel did not start until 7:30. Xiao Li took the initiative to contact the restaurant to prepare us yogurt, egg bread and oranges in advance.
Leaving the hotel in a hurry, and forgot to bring two books, Xiao Li took the initiative to send Shunfeng Express to Zhuhai.
The hotel and Xiaoli there made our Mingshi pastoral trip very comfortable and unforgettable!
